## Record Field Names, Functions and Properties

We represent field identifiers (aka. names) as strings.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="Name"></a><a id="1388" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="1393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1395" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="1399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="1404" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1406" href="Agda.Builtin.String.html#206" class="Postulate">String</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The field identifiers of a record will be stored in a sequence,
specifically Agda's `Vec` type.  We require that the field names of a
record be distinct, which we define as follows.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="distinct"></a><a id="1605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1605" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="1614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1616" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="1618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1618" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1620" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1622" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="1625" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="1627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1627" class="Bound">n</a><a id="1628" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1630" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1632" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="1636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1618" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1627" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="1640" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1642" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="1646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1605" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="1655" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#971" class="InductiveConstructor">[]</a> <a id="1658" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1660" href="Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#137" class="Record">⊤</a>
<a id="1662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1605" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="1671" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1672" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1672" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1674" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#990" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="1676" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1676" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="1678" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1680" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1682" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#535" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="1684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1672" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="1687" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Membership.Setoid.html#824" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="1689" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1676" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="1691" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1693" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Product.html#1162" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="1695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1605" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="1704" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1676" class="Bound">xs</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
For vectors of distinct elements, lookup is injective.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="distinct-lookup-inj"></a><a id="1772" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1772" class="Function">distinct-lookup-inj</a> <a id="1792" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1794" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="1796" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1797" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1797" class="Bound">n</a><a id="1798" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="1800" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1800" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="1803" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1805" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="1809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="1814" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1797" class="Bound">n</a><a id="1815" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="1817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1817" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="1819" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1819" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="1821" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1823" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1000" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="1827" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1797" class="Bound">n</a><a id="1828" class="Symbol">}</a>

We shall need to convert from an irrelevent proof of distinctness to a
relevant one. In general, this can be accomplished for any decidable
predicate. The following is a decision procedure for whether a vector
is distinct.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="distinct?"></a><a id="2546" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2546" class="Function">distinct?</a> <a id="2556" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2558" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="2560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2560" class="Bound">n</a><a id="2561" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2563" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2565" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2566" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="2569" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2571" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="2575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="2580" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2560" class="Bound">n</a><a id="2581" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2583" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2585" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#605" class="Datatype">Dec</a> <a id="2589" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2590" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1605" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="2599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2566" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="2601" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="2719" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="2724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2546" class="Function">distinct?</a> <a id="2734" class="Bound">xs</a>
<a id="2737" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="2741" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="2743" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="2747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2747" class="Bound">dxs</a> <a id="2751" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2753" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="2757" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="2759" class="Bound">x∉xs</a> <a id="2765" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2747" class="Bound">dxs</a> <a id="2771" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#209" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="2773" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="2777" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="2779" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="2782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2782" class="Bound">¬dxs</a> <a id="2787" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2789" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="2792" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="2794" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2794" class="Bound">x₁</a> <a id="2797" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2799" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2782" class="Bound">¬dxs</a> <a id="2804" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2805" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#237" class="Field">proj₂</a> <a id="2811" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2794" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="2813" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
With the decision procedure in hand, we can launder an irrelevant
proof into a relevant one.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="distinct-relevant"></a><a id="2918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2918" class="Function">distinct-relevant</a> <a id="2936" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2938" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2940" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2941" class="Bound">n</a><a id="2942" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2944" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2944" class="Bound">fs</a> <a id="2947" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2949" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="2953" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="2958" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2941" class="Bound">n</a><a id="2959" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2961" class="Symbol">.(</a><a id="2963" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2963" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="2965" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1605" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="2976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2944" class="Bound">fs</a><a id="2978" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2980" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1605" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="2991" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2944" class="Bound">fs</a>
<a id="2994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2918" class="Function">distinct-relevant</a> <a id="3012" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3013" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3013" class="Bound">n</a><a id="3014" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3016" class="Bound">fs</a><a id="3018" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3020" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3020" class="Bound">d</a>
    <a id="3026" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="3031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#2546" class="Function">distinct?</a> <a id="3041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3016" class="Bound">fs</a>
<a id="3044" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="3048" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="3050" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#641" class="InductiveConstructor">yes</a> <a id="3054" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3054" class="Bound">dfs</a> <a id="3058" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3060" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3054" class="Bound">dfs</a>
<a id="3064" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="3068" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="3070" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Relation.Nullary.html#668" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="3073" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3073" class="Bound">¬dfs</a> <a id="3078" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3080" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Empty.Irrelevant.html#327" class="Function">⊥-elimi</a> <a id="3088" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3089" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3073" class="Bound">¬dfs</a> <a id="3094" class="Bound">d</a><a id="3095" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The fields of one record are a subset of the fields of another record
if every field of the first is also a field of the second.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⊆_"></a><a id="3236" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3236" class="Function Operator">_⊆_</a> <a id="3240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3242" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="3244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3244" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="3246" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3246" class="Bound">m</a><a id="3247" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3249" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3251" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="3255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="3260" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3244" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="3262" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3264" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="3268" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="3273" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3246" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="3275" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3277" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="3281" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3281" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="3284" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3236" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="3286" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3286" class="Bound">ys</a> <a id="3289" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3291" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3292" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3292" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3294" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3296" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a><a id="3300" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3302" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3304" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3292" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3306" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Membership.Setoid.html#824" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3308" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3281" class="Bound">xs</a> <a id="3311" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3313" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3292" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3315" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Membership.Setoid.html#824" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3317" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3286" class="Bound">ys</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
This subset relation is reflexive.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊆-refl"></a><a id="3365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Function">⊆-refl</a> <a id="3372" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3374" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="3376" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3376" class="Bound">n</a><a id="3377" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3379" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3379" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="3382" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3384" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="3388" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="3393" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3376" class="Bound">n</a><a id="3394" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3396" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3398" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3379" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="3401" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3236" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="3403" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3379" class="Bound">ls</a>
<a id="3406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3365" class="Function">⊆-refl</a> <a id="3413" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3414" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3414" class="Bound">n</a><a id="3415" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3417" class="Bound">ls</a><a id="3419" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3421" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3423" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="3425" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3425" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3427" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3427" class="Bound">x∈ls</a> <a id="3432" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3434" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3427" class="Bound">x∈ls</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
It is also transitive.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="⊆-trans"></a><a id="3472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3472" class="Function">⊆-trans</a> <a id="3480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3482" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="3484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3484" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="3486" href="{% id="3507" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3509" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3509" class="Bound">ms</a>  <a id="3513" class="Symbol">:</a> <a         <a id="3553" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3555" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3491" class="Bound">ns</a> <a id="3558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3236" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="3560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3509" class="Bound">ms</a>   <a id="3565" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="3570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3509" class="Bound">ms</a> <a id="3573" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3236" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="3575" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3527" class="Bound">ls</a>
        <a id="3586" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3588" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3491" class="Bound">ns</a> <a id="3591" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3236" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="3593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3527" class="Bound">ls</a>
<a id="3596" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3472" class="Function">⊆-trans</a> <a id="3604" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3605" class="Bound">l</a><a id="3606" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3608" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link %}#3611" class="Bound">m</a><a id="3612" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3614" class="Bound">ns</a><a id="3616" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3618" class="Bound">ms</a><a id="3620" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3622" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3622" class="Bound">ls</a><a id="3624" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link id="3638" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3640" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="3642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3642" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3644" out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3632" class="Bound">ms⊆ls</a> <a id="3654" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3642" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3656" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3657" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3626" class="Bound">ns⊆ms</a> <a id="3663" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3642" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#3644" class="Bound">z</a><a id="3666" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}


If `y` is an element of vector `xs`, then `y` is at some index `i` of
the vector.

If one vector `ns` is a subset of another `ms`, then for any element
`lookup ns i`, there is an equal element in `ms` at some index.

## Types

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="4568" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="4574" class="Number">5</a> <a id="4576" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4651" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｛_⦂_｝</a>

class="Function">Name</a> <a id="4682" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4660" class="Bound">n</a><a id="4683" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4685" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4686" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4686" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="4689" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4691" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="4695" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4588" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="4700" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4660" class="Bound">n</a><a id="4701" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4703" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4705" class="Symbol">.{</a><a id="4707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4707" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="4709" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1605" class="Function">distinct</a> <a id="4720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4588" class="Datatype">Type</a> 
</pre>{% endraw %}
We do not want the details of the proof of distinctness to affect
whether two record types are equal, so we declare that parameter to be
irrelevant by placing a `.` in front of it.


## Subtyping

    <a id="5264" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5266" class="Symbol">(∀{</a><a id="5269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5269" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5271" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5273" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1000" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="5277" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5190" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5278" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5280" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="5282" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5284" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1000" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="5288" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5120" class="Bound">m</a><a id="5289" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5291" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5293" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="5300" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5123" class="Bound">ks</a> <a id="5303" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5280" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="5305" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="5307" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="5314" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5193" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="5317" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5269" class="Bound">i</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
The first premise of the record subtyping rule (`<:-rcd`) expresses
_width subtyping_ by requiring that all the labels in `ls` are also in
`ks`. So it allows the hiding of fields when going from a subtype to a
supertype.

The second premise of the record subtyping rule (`<:-rcd`) expresses
_depth subtyping_, that is, it allows the types of the fields to
change according to subtyping. The following is an abbreviation for
this premise.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="_⦂_&lt;:_⦂_"></a><a id="5932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5932" class="Function Operator">_⦂_&lt;:_⦂_</a> <a id="5941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5943" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="5945" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5946" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5946" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5953" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="5957" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#1388" class="Function">Name</a> <a id="5962" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5946" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="5964" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5966" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="5970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4588" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="5975" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5946" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="5977" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5979" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="5983" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link id="5990" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5992" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="5996" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link id="6003" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6005" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="6009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#5932" class="Function Operator">_⦂_&lt;:_⦂_</a> <a id="6018" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6019" class="Bound">m</a><a id="6020" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6022" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6022" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6023" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6025" class="Bound">ks</a> <a id="6028" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6028" class="Bound">Ss</a> <a id="6031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6031" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="6034" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6034" class="Bound">Ts</a> <a id="6037" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6039" class="Symbol">(∀{</a><a id="6042" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6042" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="6044" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6046" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1000" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="6050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6022" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6051" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6053" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6053" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6055" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6057" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Fin.Base.html#1000" class="Datatype">Fin</a> <a id="6061" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6019" class="Bound">m</a><a id="6062" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="6068" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6070" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="6077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6025" class="Bound">ks</a> <a id="6080" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6053" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6082" href="Agda.Builtin.Equality.html#125" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="6084" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="6091" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6031" class="Bound">ls</a> <a id="6094" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6042" class="Bound">i</a>  <a id="6097" class="Symbol">→</a>  <a id="6100" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="6107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6028" class="Bound">Ss</a> <a id="6110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6053" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="6112" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4957" class="Datatype Operator">&lt;:</a> <a id="6115" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="6122" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6034" class="Bound">Ts</a> <a id="6125" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6042" class="Bound">i</a><a id="6126" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
## Subtyping is Reflexive

The proof that subtyping is reflexive does not go by induction on the
type because of the `<:-rcd` rule. We instead use induction on the
size of the type. So we first define size of a type, and the size of a
vector of types, as follows.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="ty-size"></a><a id="6402" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6402" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="6410" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6412" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6413" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6413" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6415" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4588" class="Datatype">Type</a><a id="6421" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6423" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6425" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
<a id="vec-ty-size"></a><a id="6427" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6427" class="Function">vec-ty-size</a> <a id="6439" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6441" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6443" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6444" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="6446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6448" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="6449" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6451" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6453" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6454" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="6457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6459" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="6463" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4588" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="6468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6444" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6469" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6471" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6473" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#165" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="6476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6402" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="6484" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6485" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4607" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="6489" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6489" class="Bound">B</a><a id="6490" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6492" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6494" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#196" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="6498" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6402" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="6507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6485" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6509" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="6511" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6402" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="6519" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6489" class="Bound">B</a><a id="6520" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="6522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6402" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="6530" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4636" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a> <a id="6533" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6535" class="Number">1</a>

<a id="6604" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6427" class="Function">vec-ty-size</a> <a id="6616" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6617" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6618" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6620" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6621" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6621" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6623" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#990" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">∷</a> <a id="6625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6625" class="Bound">xs</a><a id="6627" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6629" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6402" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="6639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6621" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6641" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#298" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="6643" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6427" class="Function">vec-ty-size</a> <a id="6655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6625" class="Bound">xs</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
The size of a type is always positive.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="ty-size-pos"></a><a id="6707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6707" class="Function">ty-size-pos</a> <a id="6719" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6721" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6723" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6724" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6724" class="Bound">A</a><a id="6725" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6727" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6729" class="Number">0</a> <a id="6731" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#1005" class="Function Operator">&lt;</a> <a id="6733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6402" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="6741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6724" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="6743" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6707" class="Function">ty-size-pos</a> <a id="6755" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6756" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6756" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4607" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⇒</a> <a id="6760" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6760" class="Bound">B</a><a id="6761" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6763" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6765" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#960" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="6769" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#918" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a>
<a id="6773" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6707" class="Function">ty-size-pos</a> <a id="6785" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4636" class="InductiveConstructor">`ℕ</a><a id="6788" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6790" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6792" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#960" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="6796" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#918" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a>
<a id="6800" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6707" class="Function">ty-size-pos</a> <a id="6812" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4651" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｛</a> <a id="6815" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6815" class="Bound">fs</a> <a id="6818" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4651" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⦂</a> <a id="6820" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6820" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="6823" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4651" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">｝</a> <a id="6825" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6827" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6829" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#960" class="InductiveConstructor">s≤s</a> <a id="6833" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#918" class="InductiveConstructor">z≤n</a>
</pre>{% endraw %}
If a vector of types has a size smaller than `n`, then so is any type
in the vector.

{% raw %}<pre class="Agda"><a id="lookup-vec-ty-size"></a><a id="6932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6932" class="Function">lookup-vec-ty-size</a> <a id="6951" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6953" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="6955" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6955" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6956" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6958" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6958" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6959" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6961" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6962" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6962" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="6965" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6967" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#935" class="Datatype">Vec</a> <a id="6971" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#4588" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="6976" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6958" class="Bound">k</a><a id="6977" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6979" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6980" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6980" class="Bound">j</a><a id="6981" class="Symbol">}</a>
   <a id="6986" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6427" class="Function">vec-ty-size</a> <a id="7000" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6962" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="7003" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#895" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="7005" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6955" class="Bound">n</a>
   <a id="7010" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7012" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6402" class="Function">ty-size</a> <a id="7020" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7021" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Vec.Base.html#1491" class="Function">lookup</a> <a id="7028" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6962" class="Bound">As</a> <a id="7031" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6980" class="Bound">j</a><a id="7032" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7034" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/v1.1/Data.Nat.Base.html#895" class="Datatype Operator">≤</a> <a id="7036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/part2/Subtyping.md %}{% raw %}#6955" class="Bound">n</a>

</pre>{% endraw %}
Here is the proof of reflexivity, by induction on the size of the type.

## Subtyping is transitive

The proof of transitivity is straightforward, given that we've
already proved the two lemmas needed in the case for `<:-rcd`:
`⊆-trans` and `lookup-⊆`.

## Canonical Forms
